\hypertarget{raygui_8h_source}{}\doxysection{raygui.\+h}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00001\ \textcolor{comment}{/*******************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00002\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00003\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ raygui\ v4.0-\/dev\ -\/\ A\ simple\ and\ easy-\/to-\/use\ immediate-\/mode\ gui\ library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00004\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ raygui\ is\ a\ tools-\/dev-\/focused\ immediate-\/mode-\/gui\ library\ based\ on\ raylib\ but\ also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ available\ as\ a\ standalone\ library,\ as\ long\ as\ input\ and\ drawing\ functions\ are\ provided.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ FEATURES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Immediate-\/mode\ gui,\ minimal\ retained\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ +25\ controls\ provided\ (basic\ and\ advanced)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Styling\ system\ for\ colors,\ font\ and\ metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Icons\ supported,\ embeds\ a\ complete\ 1-\/bit\ icons\ pack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Standalone\ usage\ mode\ option\ (custom\ graphics\ backends)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Multiple\ tools\ provided\ for\ raygui\ development}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ POSSIBLE\ IMPROVEMENTS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Redesign\ functions\ that\ require\ a\ value\ as\ parameter\ to\ be\ returned,\ pass\ by\ reference}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Better\ standalone\ mode\ API\ for\ easy\ plug\ of\ custom\ backends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Externalize\ required\ inputs\ in\ some\ way,\ allow\ user\ customization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ LIMITATIONS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ No\ multi-\/line\ word-\/wraped\ text\ box\ support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ No\ auto-\/layout\ mechanism\ provided,\ up\ to\ the\ user\ to\ define\ controls\ position\ and\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Standalone\ mode\ requires\ library\ modification\ and\ some\ user\ work\ to\ plug\ another\ backend}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONTROLS\ PROVIDED:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Container/separators\ Controls}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ GroupBox\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/>\ Line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Panel\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/>\ StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ScrollPanel\ \ \ -\/-\/>\ StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Basic\ Controls}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ LabelButton\ \ \ -\/-\/>\ Label}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Toggle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00040\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ToggleGroup\ \ \ -\/-\/>\ Toggle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00041\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ CheckBox}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00045\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ValueBox\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/>\ TextBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00046\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Spinner\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/>\ Button,\ ValueBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Slider}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ SliderBar\ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/>\ Slider}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Advance\ Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ListView}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ ColorPicker\ \ \ -\/-\/>\ ColorPanel,\ ColorBarHue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ MessageBox\ \ \ \ -\/-\/>\ Window,\ Label,\ Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ TextInputBox\ \ -\/-\/>\ Window,\ Label,\ TextBox,\ Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ It\ also\ provides\ a\ set\ of\ functions\ for\ styling\ the\ controls\ based\ on\ its\ properties\ (size,\ color).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ RAYGUI\ STYLE\ (guiStyle):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ raygui\ uses\ a\ global\ data\ array\ for\ all\ gui\ style\ properties\ (allocated\ on\ data\ segment\ by\ default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ when\ a\ new\ style\ is\ loaded,\ it\ is\ loaded\ over\ the\ global\ style...\ but\ a\ default\ gui\ style\ could\ always\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ recovered\ with\ GuiLoadStyleDefault()\ function,\ that\ overwrites\ the\ current\ style\ to\ the\ default\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ global\ style\ array\ size\ is\ fixed\ and\ depends\ on\ the\ number\ of\ controls\ and\ properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ static\ unsigned\ int\ guiStyle[RAYGUI\_MAX\_CONTROLS*(RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_BASE\ +\ RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_EXTENDED)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ guiStyle\ size\ is\ by\ default:\ 16*(16\ +\ 8)\ =\ 384*4\ =\ 1536\ bytes\ =\ 1.5\ KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00074\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Note\ that\ the\ first\ set\ of\ BASE\ properties\ (by\ default\ guiStyle[0..15])\ belong\ to\ the\ generic\ style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00075\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ used\ for\ all\ controls,\ when\ any\ of\ those\ base\ values\ is\ set,\ it\ is\ automatically\ populated\ to\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00076\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ controls,\ so,\ specific\ control\ values\ overwriting\ generic\ style\ should\ be\ set\ after\ base\ values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ After\ the\ first\ BASE\ set\ we\ have\ the\ EXTENDED\ properties\ (by\ default\ guiStyle[16..23]),\ those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ properties\ are\ actually\ common\ to\ all\ controls\ and\ can\ not\ be\ overwritten\ individually\ (like\ BASE\ ones)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Some\ of\ those\ properties\ are:\ TEXT\_SIZE,\ TEXT\_SPACING,\ LINE\_COLOR,\ BACKGROUND\_COLOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Custom\ control\ properties\ can\ be\ defined\ using\ the\ EXTENDED\ properties\ for\ each\ independent\ control.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ TOOL:\ rGuiStyler\ is\ a\ visual\ tool\ to\ customize\ raygui\ style:\ github.com/raysan5/rguistyler}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ RAYGUI\ ICONS\ (guiIcons):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ raygui\ could\ use\ a\ global\ array\ containing\ icons\ data\ (allocated\ on\ data\ segment\ by\ default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ a\ custom\ icons\ set\ could\ be\ loaded\ over\ this\ array\ using\ GuiLoadIcons(),\ but\ loaded\ icons\ set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ must\ be\ same\ RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE\ and\ no\ more\ than\ RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS\ will\ be\ loaded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Every\ icon\ is\ codified\ in\ binary\ form,\ using\ 1\ bit\ per\ pixel,\ so,\ every\ 16x16\ icon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ requires\ 8\ integers\ (16*16/32)\ to\ be\ stored\ in\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ When\ the\ icon\ is\ draw,\ actually\ one\ quad\ per\ pixel\ is\ drawn\ if\ the\ bit\ for\ that\ pixel\ is\ set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ global\ icons\ array\ size\ is\ fixed\ and\ depends\ on\ the\ number\ of\ icons\ and\ size:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ static\ unsigned\ int\ guiIcons[RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS*RAYGUI\_ICON\_DATA\_ELEMENTS];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ guiIcons\ size\ is\ by\ default:\ 256*(16*16/32)\ =\ 2048*4\ =\ 8192\ bytes\ =\ 8\ KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ TOOL:\ rGuiIcons\ is\ a\ visual\ tool\ to\ customize/create\ raygui\ icons:\ github.com/raysan5/rguiicons}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00105\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ RAYGUI\ LAYOUT:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00106\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ raygui\ currently\ does\ not\ provide\ an\ auto-\/layout\ mechanism\ like\ other\ libraries,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00107\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ layouts\ must\ be\ defined\ manually\ on\ controls\ drawing,\ providing\ the\ right\ bounds\ Rectangle\ for\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00108\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00109\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ TOOL:\ rGuiLayout\ is\ a\ visual\ tool\ to\ create\ raygui\ layouts:\ github.com/raysan5/rguilayout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00110\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00111\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYGUI\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYGUI\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Avoid\ raylib.h\ header\ inclusion\ in\ this\ file.\ Data\ types\ defined\ on\ raylib\ are\ defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ internally\ in\ the\ library\ and\ input\ management\ and\ drawing\ functions\ must\ be\ provided\ by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ the\ user\ (check\ library\ implementation\ for\ further\ details).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYGUI\_NO\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Avoid\ including\ embedded\ ricons\ data\ (256\ icons,\ 16x16\ pixels,\ 1-\/bit\ per\ pixel,\ 2KB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYGUI\_CUSTOM\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Includes\ custom\ ricons.h\ header\ defining\ a\ set\ of\ custom\ icons,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ this\ file\ can\ be\ generated\ using\ rGuiIcons\ tool}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#define\ RAYGUI\_DEBUG\_TEXT\_BOUNDS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00130\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Draw\ text\ bounds\ rectangles\ for\ debug}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00131\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
